            FROM [dbo].[Security_Detail] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE [Extent1].[Entity_ID] IN (@p__linq__0,@p__linq__1)
        )  AS [Project1]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Security_Name] ASC
